***volk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:volk.html>volk</a> (1031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">volc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">folc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fulką</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volk.html>volk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volken.html>volken</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volkeren.html>volkeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volk.html>volkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>people, nation
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:natie.html>natie</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>tribe
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stam.html>stam</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>folk, the common people, the lower classes, the working classes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">André Hazes <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> volkszanger.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">André Hazes <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a working-class singer.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lui.html>lui</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***volley.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a> (55514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">volée</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:volta.html>volta</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">volatus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:volleys.html>volleys</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The simultaneous firing of a number of missiles or <a href = vnd.unilang:bullets.html>bullets</a>; the projectiles so fired
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1667</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="w:John Milton">John Milton</a>,  “Book 6”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Lost" class="extiw" title="w:Paradise Lost">Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a>. A Poem Written in Ten Books</a></cite>, London |  <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title=" | Printed by | ">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>  | <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Simmons" class="extiw" title="w:Samuel Simmons">Samuel Simmons</a> | ,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and are to be sold by Peter Parker under Creed Church neer Aldgate; And by Robert Boulter at the Turks Head in Bishopsgate-street; And Matthias Walker, under St. Dunstons Church in Fleet-street">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/228722708">228722708</a></small> |  republished as  <cite>Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a> in Ten Books:<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="The Text Exactly Reproduced from the First Edition of 1667: With an Appendix Containing the Additions Made in Later Issues and a Monograph on the Original Publication of the Poem">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, London |  <a href = vnd.unilang:basil.html>Basil</a> Montagu Pickering<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="196 Piccadilly">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, 1873, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/230729554">230729554</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Fiery <a href = vnd.unilang:darts.html>darts</a> in flaming <b>volies</b> flew.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>181</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Byron" class="extiw" title="w:Lord Byron">Lord Byron</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Childe_Harold%27s_Pilgrimage" class="extiw" title="w:Childe Harold | s Pilgrimage"><a href = vnd.unilang:chillen.html>Childe</a> Harold’s Pilgrimage. </a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Murray_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:John Murray (publisher)">John Murray</a>,, canto 1, stanza 38:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Each <b><a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tells.html>tells</a> that thousands cease to breathe.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harold_Edward_Bindloss" class="extiw" title="w:Harold Edward Bindloss">Harold Bindloss</a>,  chapter 30, in  <cite>The Dust of Conflict</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL4429277W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> by his order the shattered leading company flung itself into the <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> when the Sin Verguenza <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> by an enfilading <b><a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a></b> as they reeled into the <a href = vnd.unilang:calle.html>calle</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A burst or emission of many <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> at once.
<dl><dd><i>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a></i></dd>
<dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Jonson to this entry?)</span></dd>
<dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Alexander Pope to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The flight of a ball just before it bounces</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A shot in which the ball <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> played before it <a href = vnd.unilang:hits.html>hits</a> the ground
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> October 1,  John Sinnott,  “Aston <a href = vnd.unilang:villa.html>Villa</a> 2–0 Wigan”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/15045618.stm">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> nothing he could do about <a href = vnd.unilang:villa.html>Villa</a>'s second when Agbonlahor crossed from the left and <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>Bent</a> finished with a precision <b><a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sending of the ball full to the top of the wicket.</li></ol>

***vollopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vollopen.html>vollopen</a> (19082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:volmacht.html>volmacht</a> (14878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:volmacht.html>volmacht</a></i>, possibly influenced by Middle High German. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vollmacht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volmacht.html>volmacht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volmachten.html>volmachten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plenipotence, full authority or power</li>
<li>power of attorney</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:volslank.html>volslank</a> (111223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">full</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slank.html>slank</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slender</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">vollschlank</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:volstaan.html>volstaan</a> (16315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">volstaen</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vol-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">vulstān</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to persevere, guarantee, stand through</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">follastēn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand through, persevere</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<ol><li>an adult, a full-grown human or animal
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:volwassene.html>volwassene</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a>.</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vonk.html>vonk</a> (13881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vonken.html>vonke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">funko</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*funkô</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">funko</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">funcho</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Funke</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">funk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spark, touchwood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vocātus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">legal representative</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">advocātus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">witness, advocate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***voor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> (26)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vore</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fora</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fore</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furai</i>. There <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> originally two distinct Germanic forms, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furai</i> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furi</i>, which functionally merged in most Germanic languages, including Dutch. The form derived from the former became standard in Dutch, while the latter survives as the dialectal form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>for</li>
<li>before</li>
<li>in front of</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeden.html>behoeden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to protect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:middel.html>middel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">means</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbehoedsmiddel.html>voorbehoedsmiddel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbehoedsmiddelen.html>voorbehoedsmiddelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbehoedsmiddel.html>voorbehoedsmiddeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A contraceptive.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:anticonceptiemiddel.html>anticonceptiemiddel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A medical preventive, something that prevents ailments.</li></ol>

***voorbijgaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorbijgaan.html>voorbijgaan</a> (16173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vorebigaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbij.html>voorbij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass, to go by (in space or time)
<ul><li><b>1906</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Couperus" class="extiw" title="w:Louis Couperus"><a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Couperus</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensch.html>menschen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorbijgaan.html>voorbijgaan</a></i>, ch. 3:
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorde.html>hoorde</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:beneden.html>beneden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straat.html>straat</a>, Pol, <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> student; <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrienden.html>vrienden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luisterde.html>luisterde</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbijgaan.html>voorbijgaan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luidruchtige.html>luidruchtige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemmen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongelui.html>jongelui</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> her son Pol, the student, in his room; he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> smoking there with friends and she listened in <b>passing</b> to the loud <a href = vnd.unilang:voices.html>voices</a> of the youths.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
